(function ($) {
  $(document).ready(function() {
    setTimeout(function(){
      $(".displayAdx").each(function() {
        var urlPath= $(location).attr('pathname');
        var urlPathArray = urlPath.split("/");
        var validLoc = urlPathArray[1];
        var path= $(location).attr('pathname');
        var patharray = path.split("/")
        var id = $(this).attr("id");
        if (validLoc == 'locationDetail') {
          var yard = urlPathArray[2];
          var adPageName = $(this).attr("ad-page-name");
          var adPageName = adPageName + yard;
        }
        else {
          var adPageName = '';
          var adPageName = $(this).attr("ad-page-name");
        }
        var adWidth = $(this).attr("ad-width");
        var adHeight = $(this).attr("ad-height");
        var slotId = "'/35265761/"+ adPageName + "_" + adWidth + "x" + adHeight +"'";
        var styleParams = "["+adWidth + "," + adHeight +"]";
        var customDivSlotId = "'"+id+"'";
        var customSlotStr = slotId + "," + styleParams + "," + customDivSlotId;
        var s = document.createElement("script");
        var showAds = appInit.isTopBuyer;
        s.type = "text/javascript";
        var innerHtml = "try {var googletag = googletag || {};googletag.cmd = googletag.cmd || [];";
    innerHtml = innerHtml + "googletag.cmd.push(function() {var adSlotRefresh= googletag.defineSlot(" + customSlotStr + ").addService(googletag.pubads());googletag.pubads().enableSingleRequest();";
    innerHtml = innerHtml + "googletag.enableServices();googletag.display(" + customDivSlotId + ");";
    innerHtml = innerHtml + "setInterval(function(){googletag.pubads().refresh([adSlotRefresh]);}, 60000);});}catch(e){console.error(e);};";
        s.innerHTML = innerHtml;
        if((showAds != true) && (adWidth == 320)){
        $(this).append(s);
        }else if(adWidth != 320){
        $(this).append(s);
        }
      });
    }, 1000);
  });
})(jQuery);

    var trackOutboundLink = function(url) {
        ga('send', 'event', 'outbound', 'click', url, {
            'transport': 'beacon',
            'hitCallback': function(){document.location = url;}
        });
    }
</script>
